	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != '68e0e6d3a644c79112e540bff55b594e90232a8e') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '68e0e6d3a644c79112e540bff55b594e90232a8e') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'a7a54c2ee8e340cf371c2f3a0913ce73dbcfeca7') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '68e0e6d3a644c79112e540bff55b594e90232a8e') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusPagePlugin.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplusPagePlugin.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplusPagePlugin.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusPagePlugin.class.php') !== 'f0eb6d1cf0e85173d3f65cf1ad7e447291c13fae') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusPagePlugin.class.php') !== 'c3896017829194fea3dd25e28c1b564dd827d5cf') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/OIDplusPagePlugin.class.php');

			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplusPagePlugin.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusPagePlugin.class.php') !== 'f0eb6d1cf0e85173d3f65cf1ad7e447291c13fae') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusPagePlugin.class.php');

if (!is_file('includes/oidplus_base.js')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/oidplus_base.js');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('includes/oidplus_base.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/oidplus_base.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/oidplus_base.js') != 'd7c5413f9320f82b2e5790466ef8242f7767cbec') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/oidplus_base.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/oidplus_base.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/oidplus_base.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus_base.js') !== 'd7c5413f9320f82b2e5790466ef8242f7767cbec') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus_base.js') !== 'e14c027cae6b85330fc9eefd7e7269fbf9f415fa') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/oidplus_base.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/oidplus_base.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/oidplus_base.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/oidplus_base.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus_base.js') !== 'd7c5413f9320f82b2e5790466ef8242f7767cbec') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/oidplus_base.js');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: index.php');
	writefile_5();
	if (!is_file('index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('index.php') != '43def3d4eff3fa6184f52b1824c364fae955533f') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '43def3d4eff3fa6184f52b1824c364fae955533f') {
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== 'e0457b700bc8f5de5da320a7a87975236c00aa35') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '43def3d4eff3fa6184f52b1824c364fae955533f') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): index.php');
		}
	}
}
